The clinic has since expanded to Clinica San Miguel, and several other locations to better serve patients aged five and older throughout Texas.\xa0\nWhat makes Clinica San Miguel unique is its ability to care for patients through a broad selection of services, from preventive care and sick care to chronic disease management, all under one roof.\xa0\nThe physicians even have the necessary training to perform abscess drainage, electrocardiograms (EKGs), ultrasounds, and bloodwork on site.\nPatients can rest assured that the team at Clinica San Miguel can oversee all of their health care needs. Whether patients need urgent care treatment, immigration physicals, Department of Transportation (DOT) physicals, or prostate exams, the team’s state-of-the-art facility is well-equipped to meet each individual’s unique needs.\nTo schedule an appointment with one of the experienced providers at Clinica San Miguel, call or book a visit online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSchool Physicals\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEKG\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBlood Work\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSTD Testing\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDiabetes\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPap Smear\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nUltrasounds\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nVitamin B12 Injection\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAbscess Drainage\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPrimary Care\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWeight Loss\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCOVID-19 Testing\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nInternal Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWalk-In Clinic\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nHigh Blood Pressure\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPediatrics\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThyroid\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nProstate Blood Test\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDentistry\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIUD Removal\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAllergies\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\xa0\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nOur MissionOur reason for being is our patients. \nAbout\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\xa0\n\nAbout Us\n\nClinica San Miguel is a multi-specialty family medicine practice that boasts 11 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one each in Fresno, Farmers Branch,\xa0Arlington, and Pasadena.\xa0\nWith bilingual English and Spanish-speaking providers, the practice is uniquely qualified to provide comprehensive care for Hispanic communities.\nIn 2015, Clinica San Miguel’s first location launched with its Alianza Medica Hispana facility. The clinic has since expanded to Clinica San Miguel, and several other locations to better serve patients aged five and older throughout Texas.\xa0\nWhat makes Clinica San Miguel unique is its ability to care for patients through a broad selection of services, from preventive care and sick care to chronic disease management, all under one roof.\xa0\nThe physicians even have the necessary training to perform abscess drainage, electrocardiograms (EKGs), ultrasounds, and bloodwork on site.\nPatients can rest assured that the team at Clinica San Miguel can oversee all of their health care needs. Whether patients need urgent care treatment, immigration physicals, Department of Transportation (DOT) physicals, or prostate exams, the team’s state-of-the-art facility is well-equipped to meet each individual’s unique needs.\nTo schedule an appointment with one of the experienced providers at Clinica San Miguel, call or book a visit online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nTestimonials\n\n\nWords from our patients\n\n\n\n\n\n\n"The service there was AMAZING. vehicle, passing a required Department of Transportation (DOT) physical lets your employer know that you’re physically and mentally fit enough to perform your responsibilities. At Clinica San Miguel, which has 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one each in Farmers Branch,\xa0Fresno, Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena, the family medicine specialists perform DOT physicals for their patients. Call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical Q & A\n\nWhat is a DOT physical?\nA DOT physical is a comprehensive exam that evaluates your physical and mental fitness before operating a commercial motor vehicle (CMV). Individuals who operate CMVs are responsible for their safety and public safety.\nWhat happens during a DOT physical?\nMuch like a routine physical exam, a DOT physical assesses your vitals, medical history, and appearance to evaluate your overall health. The DOT physical includes:\n\nComplete physical exam\nVision test\nHearing test\nBloodwork\nUrinalysis\nUp-to-date vaccinations\nReflex, balance, and speech assessment\n\nThe team at Clinica San Miguel may order additional testing, such as a lung function test or more bloodwork, to investigate symptoms that might impact your DOT physical results.\nWhat can cause a failed DOT physical?\nFailing a DOT physical doesn’t always stop you from obtaining your clearance certification. However, you may need to return to Clinica San Miguel for additional testing to diagnose or monitor conditions such as:\n\nHigh blood pressure\nDiabetes\nEpilepsy\nMental health concerns\nCardiovascular disease\nRespiratory issues\nVision or hearing problems\n\nOther factors, such as drug or alcohol abuse, can also result in a failed DOT physical.\nWho needs a DOT physical?\nOperating a commercial vehicle requires an up-to-date DOT certification. You may need a DOT physical if you operate a vehicle:\n\nWeighing more than 10,001 pounds\nCarrying more than eight passengers for a fee\nTransporting more than 15 people\nTransporting hazardous materials\n\nYou need to have a DOT physical every two years\nHow can I prepare for a DOT physical?\nPreparing for a DOT physical can ensure a smooth process. Before your visit, make sure to bring documentation regarding any medications you’re currently taking. Valid documentation is also required if you have a disability that might prevent you from operating a commercial vehicle.\xa0\nThe team at Clinica San Miguel can help you navigate the necessary DOT physical paperwork at their office. If you’re unsure what to bring to your appointment, contact the office beforehand with any questions you may have.\nTo learn more about the DOT physical process, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore specialist provides individualized care for the whole family. At Clinica San Miguel, which has 12 locations throughout Texas — including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one apiece in Farmers Branch,\xa0Fresno, Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena — the family medicine specialists care for patients age 12 and older. To schedule an appointment with a family medicine provider, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine Q & A\n\nWhat is family medicine?\nFamily medicine is a specialty that provides regular, comprehensive care for each member of your family. With a family medicine provider on your side, your entire family can get the ongoing care they need at one facility.\nWhat makes Clinica San Miguel unique is its ability to serve a broad range of patients. The physicians provide ongoing care for individuals ages 12 and up. They also speak fluent English and Spanish, allowing them to serve Hispanic populations.\nIn addition to their high level of training and multilingual backgrounds, the team at Clinica San Miguel offers onsite bloodwork, electrocardiograms (EKGs), and other vital tests that allow their patients to receive the most comprehensive care possible under one roof.\nWhat services can family medicine specialists provide?\nFamily medicine specialists are uniquely qualified to provide all-inclusive primary care. Your primary care provider is the first doctor you see when you’re ill, due for a checkup, or in need of chronic disease management.\xa0\nThe most common services provided by the family medicine specialists at Clinica San Miguel are:\nPhysical exams\nA routine physical exam is a preventive assessment to evaluate your overall health. Most medical providers recommend visiting for a physical at least once a year to identify changes in your health and fitness.\xa0\nAlong with routine physicals, the team at Clinica San Miguel offers Department of Transportation (DOT) physicals, school physicals, and immigration physicals.\nPreventive screenings\nPreventive screenings can help identify early signs of disease. The team at Clinica San Miguel provides a full selection of common screenings, including physical exams, Pap smears, prostate exams, sexually transmitted disease (STD) testing, and bloodwork that checks for abnormal cholesterol and blood pressure levels.\nDiagnostic testing\nThe team performs a variety of diagnostic tests to investigate new or worsening symptoms. Ultrasounds, bloodwork, electrocardiograms (EKGs), and COVID-19 testing are a few of the diagnostic tests the team offers.\nAbscess drainage\nAn abscess is a pus-filled lump that typically develops from a bacterial infection. By creating an incision in the roof of the abscess, the team can drain the lesion and prevent the infection from spreading to other areas of the body.\nSick care\nIf you’re feeling unwell, the team can investigate your symptoms for an accurate diagnosis and treatment.\nWhat conditions can family medicine specialists treat?\nThe family medicine specialists at Clinica San Miguel have the qualifications and state-of-the-art equipment to treat many different conditions, including:\n\nDiabetes\nHypertension (high blood pressure)\nHigh cholesterol\nSkin lumps and bumps\nMinor injuries\nSexually transmitted diseases (STDs)\nAllergies\nThyroid disorders\nJoint disorders\n\nTo learn more about family medicine, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSchool Specialist\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel \nOur Services \nImmigration Exams\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Dallas, Farmers Branch, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nTo get your United States green card or citizenship, you need an immigration exam. The team at Clinica San Miguel performs immigration exams at its 12 locations throughout Texas: three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Farmers Branch, Fresno, Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena. These exams include testing for infectious diseases, updating vaccinations, and completing the required paperwork. To find out more about immigration exams, call the location closest to you, or book an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams Q & A\n\nWhat are immigration exams?\nU.S. Citizenship and Immigration Service (USCIS) requires immigration exams for all people seeking to register as a permanent resident or adjust status, also known as applying for your green card.\xa0\nClinica San Miguel is a full-service family medicine practice that includes physicians designated by the USCIS to perform immigration exams.\xa0\nThe purpose of the immigration exam is to make sure the person seeking a green card doesn’t have a health condition that would make them inadmissible to the US, such as an infectious disease that may be harmful to the public.\xa0\nHow do I prepare for immigration exams?\nThe Clinica San Miguel team provides specific instructions on what you need to do to prepare for your immigration exam. In general, you need to bring a valid government-issued identification (passport or driver’s license), vaccination records, and your completed USCIS health form.\xa0\nThe team may also suggest you bring a friend or family member to the appointment who can provide support, explain treatments or recommendations, or serve as a translator.\xa0\xa0\nWhat happens during immigration exams?\nImmigration exams at Clinica San Miguel aren’t like physical exams. The purpose of the exam is to assess your health and health history to make sure you don’t have any health issues that may be harmful to the public.\xa0\nYour provider at Clinica San Miguel explains what you can expect at the start of the exam. Tests are administered for a number of diseases and conditions, such as:\n\nSexually transmitted diseases (STDs) such as gonorrhea and syphilis\nLeprosy\nActive tuberculosis\nOther infectious diseases that may require quarantine\n\nThe team performs a physical exam and checks your vaccination records. They also update your vaccines as needed.\xa0\nClinica San Miguel may perform additional testing, such as bloodwork or an X-ray, and provide any necessary treatment.\xa0\nOnce you complete all of the required medical tests, your provider completes your immigration medical exam form and places it in a sealed envelope for you to include with your immigration application.\nThey also provide you with a copy of the form for your own records.\nCall Clinica San Miguel or schedule your immigration exam online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore TX\n\n\nSchool physicals are part of the admission process for many of the schools in Texas. Dedicated to meeting all of the health needs of the communities they serve, the team at Clinica San Miguel provides school physicals. The clinic has 12 locations: three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Farmers Branch,\xa0Arlington, Fresno, San Antonio, and Pasadena, Texas. Call the office nearest you or book your child’s school physical online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSchool Physicals Q & A\n\nWhat are school physicals?\nSchool physicals are medical exams required by many schools throughout Texas as part of the admission process. These physicals include a report to be completed by your provider that includes information about your child’s:\n\nGeneral health\nImmunization record\nMedical history\nHealth problems (if applicable)\nSpecial needs (if applicable)\n\nThese school physicals help make sure your child is safe and healthy for school and any extracurricular activities they might participate in. You may also need a special school physical if your child participates in sports.\nHow do I prepare for school physicals?\nSeeing children from age 12 and up, your provider at Clinica San Miguel talks to you about how you should prepare yourself and your child for their school physical.\xa0\nThe team recommends you first talk to your child about the exam and what they can expect. This helps take out some of the fear your child may have and improve their comfort level during the routine exam.\nThey also request that you bring in a list of any medications your child takes and important information about your child’s medical history and your family’s medical history.\nWhat happens during school physicals?\nThe specifics of your child’s school physical at Clinica San Miguel may depend on your child’s health needs and health changes since their last physical exam. However, a school physical is a comprehensive exam and requires more time than a sick visit.\nYour provider at Clinica San Miguel reviews your child’s medical history and asks about health concerns.\nThen they perform a physical exam that includes:\n\nHearing and vision test\nChecking height and weight\nMeasurement of temperature, blood pressure, and heart rate\nAssessment of breathing and digestion\nCheck of ears, nose, mouth, and throat\nReflex test\nEvaluation of your child’s skin, joints, and spine\n\nYour provider also reviews your child’s immunization record and provides additional vaccines as needed.\xa0\nClinica San Miguel follows the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention (CDC) vaccination schedule for children, providing vaccines as recommended based on your child’s age.\xa0\nYour provider then completes any paperwork required by your child’s school.\nTo schedule your child’s school physical, call Clinica San Miguel or book an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSchool Specialist\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel \nOur Services \nEKG\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nAn electrocardiogram (EKG) gives your doctor vital information regarding your heart health. At Clinica San Miguel, which has 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one apiece in Farmers Branch,\xa0Fresno, Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena, the family medicine specialists offer onsite EKG testing for your comfort and convenience. To learn more about EKG testing, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEKG Q & A\n\nWhat is an EKG?\nAn electrocardiogram (EKG) is a test to evaluate heart problems. The test records the electrical signals in your heart to detect abnormalities, such as arrhythmia (an abnormal heart rhythm) or blocked arteries. An EKG can also help determine whether you previously had a heart attack.\nWhy would I need an EKG?\nThe team at Clinica San Miguel may recommend an EKG if you’re displaying symptoms of heart problems, such as:\n\nHeart palpitations\nDizziness\nShortness of breath\nIncreased pulse\nFatigue\nWeakness\nLightheadedness\nChest pain\n\nHeart conditions often run in families. If you have a family history of heart disease, heart attack, or other cardiovascular disorders, an EKG gives your doctor the information they need to create an individualized heart health plan for you.\nWhat happens during an EKG?\nThe team performs EKG testing from the comfort of their office, so you don’t have to travel to an outside facility. When you arrive, you lie down on an exam table and your physician places electrodes on your chest and limbs. They may shave the area beforehand to allow better adhesion of the electrodes.\nOnce attached, the electrodes record the electrical signals in your heart and send the necessary information to an outside monitor. While it’s important to lie still during your test, you can breathe normally throughout the EKG.\nWhat happens after an EKG?\nThe team at Clinica San Miguel reviews your results with you at your appointment. Your results may indicate:\nAbnormal heart rhythm\xa0\nArrhythmias are abnormal heart rhythms that occur due to disruptions in the heart’s electrical signals.\nStructural problems\nHeart defects, enlarged heart chambers, and other problems can all cause structural abnormalities that may require additional treatment.\nAbnormal heart rate\nIf your pulse is too slow or too fast to accurately record your heart rate, the team may order an EKG to investigate the issue.\nPoor blood flow\nSymptoms like chest pain can be telltale signs of poor blood flow to the heart. An EKG can help determine whether your heart is getting the oxygen it needs to function properly.\nTo learn more about EKG testing, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSchool Specialist\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel \nOur Services \nBlood Work\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nBloodwork is an essential component of your overall health care management. At Clinica San Miguel, which has 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Farmers Branch,\xa0Fresno, Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena, the family medicine specialists offer comprehensive blood testing services. To learn more, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nBlood Work Q & A\n\nWhat is bloodwork?\nBlood tests give physicians vital information about your overall health by detecting signs of infection, disease, and chronic illness. At Clinica San Miguel, the family medicine team offers complete blood testing services to help prevent, diagnose, and manage a wide range of health conditions.\nRoutine blood tests reveal how your health changes over time. By staying up-to-date on your bloodwork, you can make educated decisions regarding your health.\nWhat are the most common types of bloodwork?\nAmong multiple types of blood tests, the most common are:\nComplete blood count (CBC)\nThe most common type of bloodwork available, a CBC tests the components within your white blood cells, red blood cells, and platelets. Levels outside the normal range can indicate an iron deficiency, nutritional deficiencies, infection, and even certain types of cancer.\nBasic metabolic panel (BMP)\nA basic metabolic panel tests several components in your blood, including calcium, sodium, and potassium, to test many of your body’s basic functions. Results from a BMP can reveal the presence of kidney disease, diabetes, and other potentially serious conditions.\nLipid panel\nA lipid panel measures the high-density lipoprotein (HDL) and low-density lipoprotein (LDL) in your blood. While HDL helps remove excess LDL, too much LDL in your blood can cause plaque to accumulate. A buildup of plaque may raise your risk of serious health complications, including stroke.\nSexually transmitted disease (STD) screening\nBlood testing can detect the presence of certain STDs, including HIV, hepatitis B, and syphilis. The earlier you know whether you have an STD, the sooner you can seek treatment.\nProstate blood test\nVisiting Clinica San Miguel for a prostate blood test can detect the early signs of prostate cancer. The screening tests the prostate-specific antigen (PSA) in your blood. Most of the PSA in the male body collects in semen, but low levels are common in the blood. High levels of PSA in the blood are a telltale sign of prostate cancer.\nWhy would I need bloodwork?\nThere are many reasons the team at Clinica San Miguel may recommend bloodwork, such as:\n\nChronic disease management\nDisease diagnosis\nPreventive care\nConfirmation of infection\nSTD detection\n\nTo learn more about bloodwork, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nSexually transmitted diseases remain a serious personal and public health issue, and knowing where to turn for comprehensive and confidential STD testing services is an important part of staying healthy. The family medicine specialists at Clinica San Miguel offer STD testing at all 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Farmers Branch,\xa0Fresno, Arlington, San Antonio, San Antonio, and Pasadena. Call today to set up a visit, or schedule online in just moments.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSTD Testing Q & A\n\nWhat are some examples of sexually transmitted diseases?\nThere are many different types of sexually transmitted diseases, some that are well-known and others you may not have ever heard of. Some of these sexually transmitted diseases include:\n\nHuman papillomavirus (HPV)\nChlamydia\nSyphilis\nBacterial vaginosis\nGonorrhea\nGenital herpes\nHepatitis\nHIV/AIDS\nTrichomoniasis\nPelvic inflammatory disease\n\nThis is far from a comprehensive list. There are dozens of different sexually transmitted diseases, which is why testing is so important.\xa0\nIt’s also essential to know that not all STDs present clear symptoms. With some infections, you may never experience easily detected changes, yet the disease could be causing serious damage to your reproductive health or immune system.\xa0\nIf you’re sexually active, getting tested is the only way to know your status. STD screening also enables you to protect others from becoming infected through sexual contact.\xa0\nWhat happens if my STD test comes back positive?\nComing in for STD screening is an easy process and takes very little time. Some tests require a blood or urine sample, while others can be diagnosed with a physical exam or a cheek swab.\xa0\nA swab of cells from your vagina, urethra, penis, cervix, or anus may be needed to determine whether you have a sexually transmitted disease. If you have blisters or sores, it may be possible to test fluid from those areas to screen for certain STDs.\nIf your STD test comes back with a positive result, your practitioner discusses all treatment options, giving you everything needed to make an informed decision about your care. Most sexually transmitted infections can be cleared up with a simple course of antibiotics. \xa0\nWhat can I do to keep from getting a sexually transmitted disease?\nThe only way to fully protect yourself from all forms of sexually transmitted disease is to avoid any form of sexual contact, including intimate touching. The next best level of protection is to remain in a mutually monogamous relationship in which both partners have been tested for sexually transmitted disease.\xa0\nUsing male or female condoms offers a high degree of protection against many forms of sexually transmitted disease, but you need to use these devices properly and during every encounter. It’s also important to understand that condoms don’t protect against all forms of sexually transmitted disease.\xa0\nIf you’re concerned about your risk level, ask your physician how you can reduce your chances of contracting an STD and enjoy an active and healthy sex life. Your provider is here to help, and there is nothing to feel ashamed or embarrassed about when it comes to your sexual health.\nIf you’d like to book an appointment for STD testing, call the office today. Online scheduling is also an option and can be done from home, any time of day or night.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily \nDiabetes\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nDiabetes is a chronic health condition that can lead to potentially harmful complications, such as neuropathy and stroke. At Clinica San Miguel, which has 12 locations throughout Texas — three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Farmers Branch,\xa0Fresno, Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena — the family medicine specialists provide comprehensive diabetes care. Managing your symptoms now can prevent complications in the future. To learn more about diabetes, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDiabetes Q & A\n\nWhat is diabetes?\nDiabetes is a long-lasting condition that occurs when your blood sugar levels are too high. The condition develops when your body produces too little of the hormone insulin or doesn’t use it efficiently. Insulin helps transport glucose (sugar) that your body uses for energy. Without insulin, sugar builds in the blood, ultimately damaging your blood vessel walls.\xa0\nManaging your blood sugar levels is crucial with diabetes. Too much sugar in the blood can damage your blood vessels and vital organs, raising your risk of cardiovascular disease, stroke, and diabetic neuropathy (nerve damage).\nAre there different types of diabetes?\nFour main types of diabetes can negatively impact your health:\nType 1 diabetes\nWhen your body doesn’t produce insulin, Type 1 diabetes may develop. Most individuals receive a diagnosis during childhood, but symptoms can develop later in life. If you have Type 1 diabetes, you must take insulin every day.\nType 2 diabetes\nType 2 diabetes typically develops in adults, but it can also occur in children and teenagers. While anybody can get Type 2 diabetes, lifestyle factors, such as poor diet, excess weight, and inactivity, significantly increase your risk.\nGestational diabetes\nGestational diabetes occurs in pregnant women. Although the condition is temporary and typically resolves after birth, gestational diabetes can increase your risk of Type 2 diabetes.\nPrediabetes\nIf your blood sugar levels are higher than normal, you may have prediabetes. Without treatment, prediabetes can evolve into Type 2 diabetes. That’s why regular physical exams and bloodwork are important steps in preventing chronic diseases, such as diabetes.\nWhat are the symptoms of diabetes?\nHow your diabetes symptoms manifest typically depends on the type you have and its progression. Common symptoms of diabetes include:\n\nDry skin\nFatigue\nSlow-healing wounds\nFrequent urination\nIncreased hunger\nUnintended weight loss\nBlurred vision\nTingling in the hands or feet\nIncreased infections\n\nDiabetes symptoms tend to worsen over time. By seeking treatment now, you can slow the disease’s progression.\nWhat causes diabetes?\nType 1 diabetes is an autoimmune disease in which your immune system attacks the cells in your pancreas that produce insulin. Physicians don’t know why the condition develops. Some of the most common causes of Type 2 diabetes include:\n\nHigh blood pressure\nA family history of diabetes\nExcess weight\nOlder age\nInactivity\nHigh cholesterol\nPolycystic ovary syndrome (PCOS)\n\nYour risk of developing Type 2 diabetes also increases if you previously had gestational diabetes during pregnancy.\nWhat are the treatments for diabetes?\nThe family medicine specialists at Clinica San Miguel offer all-inclusive care for diabetes that may include:\n\nDietary changes\nSmoking cessation\nIncreasing exercise\nMedication\nBlood sugar monitoring\nInsulin injections\n\nTo learn more about diabetes, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily women’s health screening for cervical cancer. Finding cervical cancer during the early stages improves your chances of a full recovery. At Clinica San Miguel, with 12 offices throughout Texas — three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Arlington, Farmers Branch,\xa0Fresno, San Antonio, and Pasadena — the expert team provides Pap smears. To schedule your health screening, call the office most convenient to you or book your appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPap Smear Q & A\n\nWhat is a Pap smear?\nA Pap smear, also called a Pap test, evaluates a woman’s cervical cells to look for signs of cancer. During a Pap smear, your provider uses a special tool that gently removes cells from your cervix during a pelvic exam. Then, they send the sample of cells to a lab for an evaluation.\nPap smears are often a life-saving routine health screening for women because cervical cancer is a slow-growing cancer. Pap smears help find changes to the cervical cells during the early stages when the cancer may be more responsive to treatment, improving your chance of a full recovery.\nWhen do I need a Pap smear?\nYour provider at Clinica San Miguel can advise you on how often you need a Pap smear. In general, women start Pap smears at age 21 and repeat the test every three years until age 65.\xa0\nAt age 30, you may combine your Pap smear with a human papillomavirus (HPV) test. If both are negative, you only need to repeat your Pap smear every five years.\nHPV is a sexually transmitted disease. Certain strains of HPV increase a woman’s risk of cervical cancer. If you test positive for HPV, your provider at Clinica San Miguel may recommend more frequent Pap smears.\nYou may also need more frequent Pap smears if you have a history of an abnormal test or a family history of cervical cancer.\nWhat happens during a Pap smear?\nDuring your Pap smear, you lie on your back on an exam table with your knees bent and legs spread. Your provider inserts a speculum into your vagina to gain access to your cervix. Then, they use a special tool to collect cells from your cervix.\nA Pap smear takes only a few minutes, and you may feel mild discomfort during the test. You can resume your usual activities afterward.\nWhen can I expect results from a Pap smear?\nYour provider explains when you can expect the results from your Pap smear. Once received, the clinic contacts you to share your results, which may be negative (no abnormal cells) or positive (abnormal cells).\nA positive Pap smear doesn’t mean you have cervical cancer. However, you do need additional tests to get more information about the abnormal cells found in your cervix so you can get the most effective care.\nTo schedule your Pap smear, call Clinica San Miguel or book an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore \nUltrasounds\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nUltrasounds are a great way to “see” internal body structures and understand more about how your body is functioning. Clinica San Miguel offers ultrasounds at all 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Fresno, Arlington, Farmers Branch,\xa0San Antonio, and Pasadena. If you’d like more information about the role an ultrasound might play in your health planning, book a visit online or by phone today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nUltrasounds Q & A\n\nWhat are ultrasounds?\nUltrasounds are a type of imaging that uses sound waves to create “pictures” of structures within your body. This technology uses a handheld transducer to direct high-frequency sound waves into your body.\xa0\nAs those sound waves strike internal tissues, they bounce back and are collected by the equipment. They’re translated into imaging, providing a clear and accurate view of your organs and other structures.\xa0\nHow are ultrasounds used in medical care?\nYou may be familiar with ultrasounds performed during pregnancy. The imaging created during a pregnancy ultrasound helps practitioners check a baby’s development and identify potential problems in the earliest possible stages.\xa0\nAdditional uses for medical ultrasounds include:\n\nExamining a breast lump\nChecking your thyroid gland\nEvaluating blood flow\nDiagnosing gallbladder disease\nDetecting joint inflammation\n\nThese are just some of the potential medical uses for ultrasound technology. If your physician feels that this type of imaging is a good fit for your needs, they explain the role ultrasounds can play in your diagnostic and treatment plan.\xa0\nWhat is the process for getting an ultrasound?\nOne of the reasons ultrasounds are used so frequently is that they’re safe, effective, and painless. On the day of your ultrasound, there’s no need for any form of anesthesia.\nDepending on the area being examined, you may be asked to refrain from eating or drinking for a period of time prior to your visit. You might also be asked to drink a lot of water to enhance bladder imaging.\xa0\nMost ultrasounds are performed using a handheld transducer that is moved across the surface of your skin. Some types use a probe inserted into your vagina or anus to create the required imaging.\xa0\nFor external ultrasounds, the practitioner applies a clear gel to your skin to help the transducer glide over the surface of your skin and to enhance sound wave transmission. Depending on the area your doctor is attempting to view, you might need to alter your position during the ultrasound. The entire process usually takes less than 30 minutes.\xa0\nThe imaging created during an ultrasound is transmitted onto an external screen. Your practitioner can see those images as the ultrasound is being performed, and can determine if additional screening is needed.\xa0\nBooking a visit for an ultrasound at Clinica San Miguel takes just moments online or by phone, so don’t delay.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration You don’t produce your own supply of this vitamin; it comes from food sources.\xa0\nFoods like meat, fish, poultry, and dairy products all contain vitamin B12. Some grain products and other foods are fortified with vitamin B12. While true vitamin B12 deficiency is low among Americans, those who embrace a plant-based diet can develop a deficiency because plant foods don’t provide this essential nutrient.\xa0\nWhat are some signs that I might have a vitamin B12 deficiency?\nKnowing what to look for can help you decide when to seek treatment for vitamin B12 deficiency. Some of the symptoms that indicate a vitamin B12 deficiency include:\n\nFatigue\nAnemia\nWeakness\nDifficulty walking normally\nSensations of numbness or weakness in your hands, legs, or feet\nSwollen, inflamed tongue\n\nIf you notice any of these changes, schedule a visit at Clinica San Miguel right away. A thorough diagnostic examination can help determine the source of your symptoms. If it appears you have a vitamin B12 deficiency, a series of vitamin B12 injections can be a great treatment option.\xa0\nHow can vitamin B12 injections improve my health and wellness?\nA series of vitamin B12 injections can correct an existing vitamin B12 deficiency. While you can get all of the vitamin B12 you need through food sources, it takes time to increase your levels through food alone.\xa0\nYou can also take oral supplements or a multivitamin to increase your vitamin B12 levels, but research shows that a portion of many supplements pass completely through your digestive system without being broken down or absorbed.\xa0\xa0\nVitamin B12 injections allow you to quickly boost your levels in a way that is safe and effective. Under the care of a skilled medical professional, these injections are a great way to supplement your other health and wellness efforts.\xa0\nYou might begin to feel the positive effects right away, but it can take weeks for your body to truly benefit from a round of vitamin B12 injections.\xa0\nIf you’d like more information, call the practice today to book a visit, or schedule using the easy Drainage\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nAn abscess is an infected or inflamed area of the skin that causes a large, pus-filled lump to form. At Clinica San Miguel, which has 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Fresno, Arlington, Farmers Branch,\xa0San Antonio, and Pasadena, the family medicine specialists offer prompt care for abscesses. Abscess drainage is a safe and effective technique to treat these painful bumps. To learn more about abscess drainage, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAbscess Drainage Q & A\n\nWhat is abscess drainage?\nAn abscess is a pus-filled lump that forms beneath an inflamed area of the skin. Most abscesses form from bacterial infections and can develop nearly anywhere on the body, particularly in the extremities.\xa0\nSmall abscesses often disappear on their own, but larger lumps may require professional treatment. Abscess drainage involves puncturing the lump to remove its pus. Once the pus drains, the abscess is more likely to heal on its own.\nWhat happens during abscess drainage?\nWhen you arrive for your appointment, the family medicine team at Clinica San Miguel cleans and sterilizes the treatment area to prevent infection. Next, they administer a local anesthetic to ensure your comfort throughout the procedure.\nTo perform the drainage, your physician makes a careful incision toward the top of the abscess with a thin needle. Pus then drains out of the abscess pocket, which the team cleans with a sterile solution.\nDepending on the size of the abscess, the team may leave the abscess open or place space inside the pocket to keep it open. Finally, they cover the abscess with a wound dressing to protect it and absorb any additional pus.\nHow can I prepare for abscess drainage?\nYou should avoid touching your abscess before your appointment to avoid complications. In many instances, the team at Clinica San Miguel prescribes antibiotics beforehand to treat the infection. A course of antibiotics also prevents the infection from spreading to other areas of the body.\nCan I perform abscess drainage myself?\nWhile it may be tempting to try draining an abscess yourself, doing so can have serious consequences. Only a qualified physician has the necessary training to perform abscess drainage without spreading the infection or damaging your skin.\nWhat is the recovery like after abscess drainage?\nMost patients can drive themselves home after the procedure. However, if the abscess is on your leg, it can impair your ability to drive. The abscess typically continues to drain pus and fluid after the procedure.\xa0\nIt’s important to change your wound dressing once the fluid soaks through it. Pus can continue to drain for up to two days after you return home.\nIf the team suspects you have an infection, they may prescribe antibiotics after the procedure. Pain medication may also be available to relieve any discomfort you experience while you heal.\nTo learn more about abscess drainage, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSchool They perform all of your wellness exams, and they're the first person you see when you’re sick.\xa0\nEveryone needs a primary care provider. Clinica San Miguel is a family medicine practice that offers primary care services for people of all ages, including pediatrics. They also provide primary care for men’s and women’s health.\xa0\nWhat are primary care services?\nClinica San Miguel covers all of your health needs through their primary care services. These services include:\nAnnual physical exams\nPrimary care focuses on health promotion and disease prevention. Your annual physical exam is one of the most important visits with your primary care provider.\xa0\nIt gives your provider at Clinica San Miguel an opportunity to assess your current health and look for future health problems.\nIn addition to annual physicals, Clinica San Miguel performs Department of Transportation (DOT) physicals, immigration physicals, and school physicals.\nDiagnostic tests\nClinica San Miguel also provides many types of diagnostic tests to assess health and diagnose health problems. Testing includes bloodwork, ultrasounds, and electrocardiograms (EKG). Clinica San Miguel also provides COVID-19 testing.\nUrgent care\nTo manage your unexpected health issues, Clinica San Miguel offers urgent care. The team specializes in diagnosing and treating many chronic diseases such as diabetes, high blood pressure, and thyroid problems.\nWhat can I expect during a primary care appointment?\nYou can expect patient-focused care during a primary care appointment at Clinica San Miguel. They review your health concerns, perform a physical exam, run any tests or health screenings, and provide necessary treatments.\nYour primary care provider also talks to you about your health and the things you can do to improve your current health and prevent future health problems.\xa0\nFor primary care services that focus on you, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nAre you ready to try a new approach to weight loss that doesn’t rely on fad diets and extreme exercise programs? If so, medically supervised weight loss is a great option, and it’s one of many services available at Clinica San Miguel, with 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one apiece in Fresno, Farmers Branch,\xa0Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena. Many factors contribute to becoming overweight or obese. What researchers do know is that weight gain is not a simple matter of willpower.\xa0\nThe American food supply is partially to blame. Highly processed foods line grocery store shelves, and fast food is readily available in every city and town in the nation.\xa0\nOur modern lifestyle is also a leading cause of overweight and obesity. More time spent sitting in front of screens at home, at school, and at work leaves little time for getting outside for fresh air and exercise. High levels of anxiety and depression and poor sleep quality also play a role in weight gain.\xa0\nWhat are the health risks of being overweight or obese?\nCarrying a significant amount of extra weight is one of the most damaging things to overall health and wellness. Some of the health risks associated with being overweight or obese include:\n\nHeart disease\nStroke\nType 2 diabetes\nGallbladder disease\nHigh blood pressure\nHigh cholesterol\nSleep apnea\nOsteoarthritis\nDepression and anxiety\nCognitive issues\nSexual dysfunction\n\nAs you can see, being overweight or obese takes a toll on virtually every organ and system in your body. If you’ve been diagnosed with a chronic health issue, you’ve likely been advised to lose weight as part of your treatment process.\xa0\nHow is medically supervised weight loss different?\nIf you’re like many people, you’ve tried many different diet and exercise plans over the years. You may even have had a degree of success, only to see the weight quickly return once you stop your diet and exercise efforts.\xa0\nMedically supervised weight loss is different because it begins with a central focus on your health. Your weight loss plan is devised to align with your current health strengths and weaknesses.\xa0\nUnlike many popular exercise programs, you’re not pushed to extremes that can threaten your musculoskeletal system.\xa0\nMedications might play a role in your weight loss journey. While drug therapy can help control appetite and alter the way you convert food into energy, the primary focus is on establishing meaningful lifestyle modifications that can help you reach and maintain a healthy weight over the long term.\xa0\nYou have the support of the Clinica San Miguel team as you move closer to your ideal weight. You also have people to hold you accountable, which can help keep you on track to reach your goals.\nWhen you’re ready to learn more, call the office to set up a consultation, or schedule online.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration Exams\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nSchool Specialist\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel \nOur Services \nCOVID-19 Testing\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nCOVID-19 testing is an essential step in preventing the spread of the SARS-CoV-2 virus. At Clinica San Miguel, which has 12 locations throughout Texas, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Fresno, Arlington, Farmers Branch,\xa0San Antonio, and Pasadena, the family medicine specialists offer fast, accurate COVID-19 testing to help you make informed decisions about your health. The earlier you know whether you have the virus, the sooner you can take the appropriate next steps. Call Clinica San Miguel today or book an appointment online to learn more.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nCOVID-19 Testing Q & A\n\nWhat is COVID-19 testing?\nCOVID-19 is a potentially serious infection caused by the SARS-CoV-2 virus. Testing for COVID-19 detects the presence of the virus or the antibodies that develop once you build up immunity to it. Antibodies can also develop after you receive your COVID-19 vaccine.\nAre there different types of COVID-19 testing?\nViral tests detect the presence of COVID-19 in the saliva. There are currently two types of viral tests available:\xa0\nLaboratory tests\nLaboratory testing is the most accurate way to detect the presence of COVID-19. These tests include reverse transcription-polymerase chain reaction (PCR) and nucleic acid amplification tests (NAATs).\nDuring this test, the team at Clinica San Miguel takes a saliva sample from your mouth or a deep nasal swab inside your nose and sends it to the lab. Results are typically available within 1-2 days.\xa0\nRapid tests\nRapid tests include antigen and some types of NAATs. After the team collects your saliva sample, results are typically available within one day.\nAntibody testing, or serology testing, detects the presence of SARS-CoV-2 antibodies in your blood. Your immune system creates antibodies to fight infection. By searching for antibodies, this test can indicate past infection.\nWhen do I need COVID-19 testing?\nYou should visit Clinica San Miguel for a COVID-19 test if you’ve recently come into contact with an infected individual. It’s also important to seek testing when you’re showing signs of infection yourself.\xa0\nMany individuals are required to show proof of a negative test before certain events, such as work functions, sporting events, or air travel.\nHow do I know if I need COVID-19 testing?\nInvestigating the signs of COVID-19 is essential to determine whether you have the infection. Common COVID-19 symptoms include:\n\nPersistent cough\nSore throat\nHeadache\nLost sense of taste or smell\nFatigue\nChills\nBody or muscle aches\nWheezing\nTrouble breathing\n\nWithout treatment, COVID-19 symptoms can worsen. The earlier you seek testing, the more likely you are to recover without complications.\nWhy is COVID-19 testing important?\nThe Centers for Disease Control and Prevention (CDC) reports that there have been more than 50 million cases of COVID-19 just in the United States. That number only grows without prompt, accurate testing.\xa0\nBy seeking COVID-19 testing as soon as you develop symptoms or come in contact with an infected individual, you can take the appropriate precautions to prevent the spread.\nTo learn more about COVID-19 testing, call Clinica San Miguel or schedule an appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Internal medicine physicians undergo years of education and training so they can diagnose and treat any health condition that affects adults.\xa0\nInternal medicine physicians are also experts in health promotion and disease prevention. They\xa0 manage general health and provide health screenings and education that might prevent or delay health problems.\xa0\nInternal medicine physicians also have the ability to diagnose and treat acute and chronic health conditions, ranging from a simple cold or a complex health problem like diabetes.\nWhat are internal medicine services?\nClinica San Miguel is dedicated to providing comprehensive health services to the communities they serve. The internal medicine team at Clinica San Miguel provides many health services for adults, including:\nAnnual physical exams\nYour annual physical exam is the most important health exam of the year. This exam gives your internal medicine physician at Clinica San Miguel an opportunity to evaluate your whole health.\nIt also gives you a chance to discuss any health concerns you may have. After your physical, your doctor makes recommendations to promote health and prevent disease.\nUrgent care\nThe internal medicine team at Clinica San Miguel also provides urgent care, managing all of your unexpected health issues, such as a cold or flu, sprain or strain, or a minor cut.\nInternal medicine physicians train in critical care and understand how to quickly and effectively treat unexpected health problems.\nHealth screenings\nHealth screenings find health problems before they become serious health complications. Clinica San Miguel provides health screenings to check for conditions like diabetes, high blood pressure, and high cholesterol.\xa0\nThe clinic also offers Pap smears for women to screen for cervical cancer and prostate blood tests for men to screen for prostate cancer.\xa0\nCan internal medicine manage my chronic health problems?\nThe internal medicine team at Clinica San Miguel diagnoses, treats, and monitors simple and complex chronic diseases. It’s a great fit for medical issues that need to be seen promptly but don’t necessarily require an emergency room setting.\xa0\nOne way to think about urgent care is to consider whether your need can wait to be treated during a normally scheduled appointment at Clinica San Miguel. If you’re in pain or are worried about troubling symptoms, an urgent care visit might be the best course of action.\nWhat kinds of issues can be treated in a Walk-in Clinic?\nClinica San Miguel has highly skilled practitioners who can address a wide range of medical needs. Some of the issues frequently seen in walk-in visits include:\n\nFever\nSore throat\nCold and flu symptoms\nStrains and sprains\nMinor cuts and abrasions\nHeadache\nSkin rash\nAllergic reactions\n\nThe Walk-in Clinic is a great way to get high-quality medical care in a time frame that fits your needs.\xa0\nHow do I know if I should go to urgent care or the emergency room?\nSome medical needs are best met in an emergency room, where physicians trained in emergency medicine are standing by to provide life-saving treatment for severe health issues.\xa0\nHowever, if you don’t need the specialized equipment or services available in the emergency room, you may want to look elsewhere for urgent care.\xa0\nEmergency room staff members quickly assess your condition and prioritize patients who have serious medical emergencies. If your needs don’t rise to the level of a true emergency, you can find yourself waiting for hours before you’re seen by a doctor. You spend that time in a waiting room filled with people who might have various viruses or other infections.\xa0\nHere are some conditions that should be seen in an emergency room:\n\nChest pain\nBreathing difficulties\nLoss of consciousness\nUncontrollable bleeding\nSevere asthma attack\nSevere allergic reaction\nBroken bones that break through the skin\nSymptoms of stroke\n\nIf your needs don’t appear life-threatening, call Clinica San Miguel to determine if a Walk-in Clinic visit is appropriate. Online booking is available for routine care needs.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore Services \nHigh Blood Pressure\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nHigh blood pressure is a common chronic health problem that develops without causing symptoms. When left untreated, high blood pressure increases your risk of having a heart attack or stroke. The team at Clinica San Miguel provides comprehensive care for high blood pressure, improving numbers and overall health. Clinica San Miguel has 12 clinics, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one in Fresno, Arlington, Farmers Branch,\xa0San Antonio, and Pasadena, Texas. Call or book an appointment online at the clinic closest to you today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nHigh Blood Pressure Q & A\n\nWhat is high blood pressure?\nHigh blood pressure, also known as hypertension, is a chronic health condition that affects the walls of your blood vessels. Blood pressure measures the force of blood against the blood vessel walls, which is highest when your heart beats.\nHigh blood pressure means the force is too high. Over time, excess pressure causes your blood vessels to stiffen and narrow, making your heart work harder to pump the blood.\xa0\nThe condition also increases your risk of developing other health conditions, such as heart disease and kidney disease. Further, it puts you at risk of having a heart attack or stroke.\nHow do I know if I have high blood pressure?\nHigh blood pressure is often referred to as the “silent killer” because it develops without causing symptoms. The only way to know if you have high blood pressure is by getting your blood pressure evaluated.\nClinica San Miguel is a family medicine practice committed to providing comprehensive care to the communities they serve. They offer all general health services, including primary care services, annual physical exams, and treatment for unexpected illnesses and injuries.\nEvery time you come in for care, the Clinica San Miguel team checks your blood pressure. One higher-than-normal blood pressure reading doesn’t mean you have high blood pressure.\xa0\nHowever, if your provider has concerns about your readings, they may recommend that you monitor your numbers at home or have you come to the clinic for periodic blood pressure checks.\xa0\nYour provider may diagnose you with high blood pressure if you have elevated blood pressure readings on three separate office visits.\nHow is high blood pressure treated?\nTreatment for high blood pressure may include lifestyle changes, medication, or both. Your provider at Clinica San Miguel customizes your treatment plan based on your blood pressure readings and related health complications.\nLifestyle changes that can help lower your blood pressure include:\n\nLimiting salt in your diet\nEating more fruits and vegetables\nGetting regular exercise\nWeight loss\nSmoking cessation\n\nThe team may also prescribe blood pressure medication to help you lower your numbers and improve your health.\nYou can get control over your high blood pressure when you have a team of health professionals dedicated to improving your health and well-being. Call Clinica San Miguel or schedule your high blood pressure appointment online today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily \nThyroid\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nLiving with a thyroid condition can cause widespread health issues. Help is available from the team of highly skilled practitioners at Clinica San Miguel, which has three locations in Dallas, five Houston, and one apiece in Fresno, Farmers Branch,\xa0Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena, Texas. If you’re concerned about changes in your overall health and would like to be screened for a thyroid condition, schedule a visit online or by phone today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nThyroid Q & A\n\nWhat is the thyroid and what does it do in the body?\nYour thyroid is a small organ located at the front of your throat, just beneath your Adam’s apple. Shaped like a butterfly, your thyroid extends around to the sides of your throat.\xa0\nThe thyroid is a gland that produces hormones that deliver chemical messages throughout the body, prompting all kinds of cellular functions. Your thyroid manufactures thyroid hormones, which regulate your metabolism. This relatively tiny gland within your body has a very large role in how you convert food into energy.\xa0\nWhat are some common thyroid conditions?\nThere are two main types of thyroid disorders: hyperthyroidism and hypothyroidism.\xa0\nHyperthyroidism\nThis condition occurs when your thyroid gland produces too many thyroid hormones. Symptoms include:\n\nRestlessness\nTremors\nSleep disruption\nThinning skin\nSweating\nIntolerance to heat\nFrequent bowel movements\nRapid heart rate\nUnexplained weight loss\n\nHypothyroidism\nThis condition occurs when your thyroid gland doesn’t produce enough thyroid hormones. Symptoms include:\n\nFatigue\nHair loss\nFeeling cold\xa0\nDepression\xa0\nConstipation\nMemory problems\nHigh cholesterol\nExtremely dry skin\n\nIf you notice these changes, schedule a diagnostic exam to determine if a thyroid disorder is to blame.\xa0\nWhat are some treatment options for thyroid issues?\nIf you’re diagnosed with hypothyroidism, the primary treatment is to supplement your natural thyroid hormone production with a synthetic option.\xa0\nPeriodic blood testing helps determine if you’re getting the right volume of medication to keep symptoms at bay. Most people with hypothyroidism need medication for the rest of their lives.\xa0\nIf you have hyperthyroidism, you have several treatment options. Drug therapy can slow your natural thyroid hormone production, and another option is radioactive iodine, which works by destroying a portion of your thyroid cells.\xa0\nBeta-blockers are often prescribed along with thyroid medication or radioactive iodine to slow your heart rate and prevent heart palpitations.\xa0\nFor those who aren’t good candidates for these treatments, surgery can remove a portion of your thyroid, but you’ll likely need to take supplemental synthetic thyroid hormones for the rest of your life to achieve optimal balance.\xa0\nFor more information about thyroid disorders and treatment paths, schedule a visit at Clinica San Miguel online or over the phone today.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore Services \nProstate Blood Test\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nA prostate blood test, or PSA test, measures how much prostate-specific antigen is in your blood to screen your risk for prostate cancer. Get this test from the qualified medical team at Clinica San Miguel. Call one of the three offices in Dallas, five in Houston, or one each in Fresno, Pasadena, Farmers Branch,\xa0San Antonio, or Arlington, Texas, to schedule your prostate blood test, or use the online tool to book.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nProstate Blood Test Q & A\n\nWhat is a prostate blood test?\nA prostate blood test, or PSA test, assesses a man’s risk of prostate cancer. The prostate is a small gland — about the size and shape of a walnut — that produces seminal fluid to support and transport sperm.\xa0\nProstate cancer is common, but it’s slow-growing and often confined to the prostate gland. Some forms, however, can be more aggressive and may spread quickly. This may endanger other organs and even your life. More than 34,000 men die of prostate cancer yearly.\xa0\nCancerous and noncancerous tissue in your prostate produces PSA (prostate-specific antigen). The PSA test detects high levels of PSA that may indicate cancerous tissue.\xa0\nHigh levels of PSA don’t always mean cancer, however. It can also indicate inflammation or enlargement of the organ.\xa0\nYou may also need a prostate blood test if you’ve been diagnosed with cancer. It can judge the effectiveness of your treatment plan and check for recurring cancer.\xa0\nWho should get a prostate blood test?\nPSA tests are recommended to start at age 55 for most healthy males with no history of prostate cancer in their family or themselves. Men aged 40-54 may benefit from a PSA test if prostate cancer runs in the family or their ethnicity has a higher risk of developing aggressive cancers.\xa0\nWhat are the benefits of getting a prostate blood test?\nCancer is much easier to treat and cure when detected early. You have a better chance of full remission and no spread when a PSA test helps you find early cancerous growth on your prostate.\nA prostate blood test may be done along with a digital rectal exam. If high levels of PSA are found and the digital rectal exam shows evidence of possible cancer, your provider may recommend a prostate biopsy.\xa0\nIf cancer is detected, the team at Clinica San Miguel can get you started with cancer treatment right away.\xa0\nWhat happens during a prostate blood test?\nA prostate blood test involves a simple blood draw from a vein, most likely in your arm. The team then sends this sample to a lab for evaluation.\xa0\nYou’re notified of your results and whether your doctor recommends further testing or a prostate biopsy.\xa0\nContact the most convenient location of Clinica San Miguel to schedule your prostate blood test. \nDentistry\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nYour oral health is a critical part of your overall well-being. Without good dental care, you risk tooth decay, tooth loss, gum disease, and other complications. At the North West Dallas, Texas, location of Clinica San Miguel, you get the dental care you need to have healthy teeth and gums and a great smile. Call the office today to schedule an appointment, or use the online tool to book. \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nDentistry Q & A\n\nWhat is involved in dentistry care?General dentistry includes all care and treatment to keep your teeth, gums, and other oral structures healthy. Dentistry includes preventive care, like routine exams and cleanings as well as oral cancer screenings. The dental team at Clinical San Miguel can help treat minor gum disease and fill cavities too.\xa0Other important procedures that dentistry care can help with include:Root canalsDental implantsCustom mouthguardsFillings and crownsProfessional teeth whiteningThe team at Clinical San Miguel can also do extractions if you should have a painful tooth that can’t be saved.\xa0How often do I need dentistry care?Your oral health is important to the health of your entire body. Tooth or gum infections can cause inflammation in other parts of your body and contribute to poor quality of life.\xa0Patients with good at-home dental care and who are in generally good health need to see their dentist for a routine visit every six months. The team uses these routine exams to help keep your teeth and gums healthy, in addition to checking for early warning signs of oral cancer, problems with wisdom teeth, or the occasional cavity.\xa0People with gum disease or tooth decay may require more frequent visits. If you have a severe toothache or other tooth complication, schedule an appointment between your routine visits.\xa0What happens during a dental exam?During your routine dental visit, the team thoroughly cleans your teeth. Your hygienist can reach areas that just aren’t possible to reach with a normal toothbrush at home. They also get under the gumline to help keep gum disease away.\xa0Trust your hygienist to:Evaluate the health of your gums, tongue, and throatClean each tooth one by oneTake new X-ray imagesFloss between teethTeach you proper brushingAfter your teeth cleaning, the dentist reviews your X-rays and checks each tooth for signs of damage or decay.\xa0Get the dental care you need to preserve a healthy smile. \nIUD Removal\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nAn intrauterine device (IUD) is a popular contraceptive option because it protects a woman from getting pregnant without having to take pills, receive injections, or use accessories. When it’s time to remove your IUD, whether it’s because you want to get pregnant or because the IUD has expired, contact Clinical San Miguel. With 12 locations in Texas — five in Houston, three in Dallas, and one in Arlington, Pasadena, Farmers Branch,\xa0San Antonio, and Fresno — you get compassionate providers who can perform this procedure quickly in-office. Call today or use the online tool to schedule your IUD removal.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nIUD Removal Q & A\n\nWho should get their IUD removed?\nDon’t try to remove an IUD yourself. Removal should always be done in a clinical setting. You risk infection and damage to your internal organs if you try to pull the IUD out by yourself.\xa0\nGet your IUD removed if it has expired. IUDs protect you from pregnancy for 3-10 years, depending on the type you have. Copper IUDs (ParaGuard®) last 10 years, while progestin IUDs (Kyleena®, Liletta®, Mirena®, and Skyla®) work for 3-5 years.\xa0\nOther reasons to remove your IUD:\n\nYou want to get pregnant\nThe IUD is causing serious side effects like pain or heavy bleeding\nYour IUD has moved or broken\nYou have a sexually transmitted infection\n\nAn IUD is 99% effective in preventing pregnancy, but if you do accidentally get pregnant with an IUD in place, you should have it removed.\xa0\nWhat is it like to undergo IUD removal?\nThe IUD removal process takes just a few minutes. You change into a dressing gown and lie on an exam table with your knees bent and legs open.\xa0\nYour provider places a speculum in your vagina to hold open the walls. They use a special grasping tool to take hold of the strings of your IUD and gently pull the IUD out. The T-shaped IUD folds as it slides from your uterus.\xa0\nIf the threads of your IUD aren’t easily seen, your provider uses a special tool to pull them into view.\xa0\nIn rare cases, the IUD can get stuck to the wall of your uterus. In these cases, you may need a more in-depth procedure that requires medication to dilate your cervix and forceps to pull the IUD out. You receive pain medication to make this procedure more comfortable.\xa0\nWhat happens after IUD removal?\nYou may feel cramps and light spotting or bleeding for a few days or weeks following IUD removal.\xa0\nYou can opt to get a new IUD the same day as one is removed. If you want to get pregnant, you can start trying right away.\xa0\nSchedule your IUD removal at Clinica San Miguel. Call one of the 11 locations today, or use the online tool to plan your visit.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore \nAllergies\n\n\n\n\n\nTweet\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nClinica San Miguel\nFamily Medicine located in San Antonio, Farmers Branch, Dallas, Houston, Arlington, Fresno, & Pasadena, TX\n\n\nAccording to the Asthma and Allergy Foundation of America, as many as 50 million Americans experience some form of allergic reaction each year. Those in Texas can rely on Clinica San Miguel for relief, with 12 locations throughout the state, including three in Dallas, five in Houston, and one each in Fresno, Farmers Branch,\xa0Arlington, San Antonio, and Pasadena. Don’t suffer from allergy symptoms when help is available. Call or click today to book a personalized visit.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nAllergies Q & A\n\nWhat are allergies?\nAllergies are actually an impressive display of your body’s natural immune function. That said, it’s difficult to appreciate your innate immune function when you’re dealing with symptoms of an allergic reaction.\nAllergies occur when your immune system mistakenly launches a strong attack against a substance (allergen) that is not typically harmful to humans. Your body creates antibodies to fight off an infection, the same way that your system works after getting a vaccine.\xa0\nWhen this response happens after exposure to a harmless substance, however, your body will create symptoms every time you encounter that substance in the future. This is why allergies are so disruptive.\xa0\nWhat are some common allergens?\nMany different substances can trigger an allergic reaction. Some people are only sensitive to one or two allergens, while others experience an allergic reaction when exposed to numerous substances. The team at Clinica San Miguel can help you determine the root cause of reactions you may be experiencing.\nSome common allergens include:\n\nPollen\nDust mites\nPet dander\nShellfish\nHousehold chemicals\nGrass\nEggs\nBee stings\nLatex\nPenicillin\nMold\n\nThese are just some of the allergens that can trigger an allergic reaction. If you experience allergy symptoms like sudden swelling, skin changes, breathing difficulties, or stomach pain, reach out to Clinica San Miguel to schedule a diagnostic exam.\nWhat can be done to treat allergies?\nThe family medicine specialists at Clinica San Miguel can help you learn which substances provoke an attack so you can take steps to avoid exposure. This is easier with allergens like cigarette smoke or latex but very challenging with others like pollen, dust mites, or foods.\xa0\nImmunotherapy is an excellent option for treating allergies. The process works by exposing your immune system to small volumes of allergens to develop a tolerance. Over time, your immune system will react less intensely when encountering that allergen in full strength. Your provider may also prescribe certain medications to ease your allergy symptoms, in the form of pills, eye drops, nasal sprays, or liquids.\xa0\nThe team at Clinica San Miguel believes that everyone deserves access to top-quality care and is proud to deliver consistent, compassionate care to the Hispanic community. If you’d like to be tested for allergies or are searching for a new treatment path, call Clinica San Miguel to set up a visit. Online booking is also an option and takes just moments to complete.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore     \n\n\n        Additional Services\n      \n\n\n        General Consultation\n      \n\n\n\n\xa0\n\nLa\xa0General medecine\xa0it is the branch of medicine that is responsible for attending to most of the demands and pathologies of patients. It is usually in most cases the first contact of the patient with the health system. Therefore, the general practitioner, or family doctor, must have a wide range of knowledge to try to give an adequate response or refer to the appropriate specialist.At the\xa0San Miguel Clinic\xa0we have an excellent team of professionals who make up primary care or general medicine\xa0capable of treating a wide range of ailments..\xa0In general, we should all go to medical consultations periodically to preserve our well-being.\xa0Medical check-ups help us stay in top shape and take care of ourselves.People with diabetes or high cholesterol should come to have their sugar and cholesterol levels checked. Other reasons can be:Tratamiento de los resfriados o gripes comunes.Tratamiento de la gastroenteritis o problemas estomacales.Treatment of Cholesterol, Pressure, Thyroid, Diabetes, Allergies.\xa0Chronic Pain.Sexually transmitted diseases.InfectionsThe general practitioner will also help us to take preventive measures against some diseases. Giving us keys to take care of our health when we are in old age, during pregnancy or at any other stage of our life.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore designated by the US Department of State (also known as a “panel physician”).There are certain types of illnesses and medical conditions that doctors will be looking for:\xa0-Gonorrhea.-Infectious leprosy.-Infectious syphilis.-Active tuberculosis.- Diseases that are susceptible to quarantine.-Diseases that put public health at risk.Also the doctor in charge must ensure that it complies with the vaccinations required by the United States. drive a commercial vehicle without any impeding medical conditions that put yourself or others on the road at risk.Blood pressureSight and hearingLung, spine, and limb functionMouth and throatBalance and reflexesUrinary systemThere will also be a section that will review your medical history. Here are some of the categories your medical history will address:Blood pressure and heart healthSight and hearing\xa0History of dizziness, fainting spells, strokes, and respiratory healthDrug and alcohol useHistory of diabetes or other specific diseasesBrain injuries and / or psychiatric disorders\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore students to submit to a school physical. The school physical report is a document for the school to obtain a general picture of the student's health, immunizations, medical history and, if necessary, any major health problems or special needs.We suggest doing the following to help you and your child prepare for their physical exam before returning to school:Talk to your child about what will happen during the physical exam to help him feel comfortable.Write a list of family medical history to share with the provider.Bring a list of any medications your child is currently taking.Comment on any changes you have noticed in your child's health since his last checkup.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily Medicine\nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nImmigration  \n\n\n        Additional Services\n      \n\n\n        Electrocardiogram\n      \n\n\n\n\xa0\n\nAn EKG records the electrical signals from the heart. It is a common and painless test used to detect heart problems.An EKG is a painless and non-invasive way to diagnose many common heart problems in people of all ages. Your doctor may use an EKG to determine or detect:An abnormal heart rhythm (arrhythmias).If clogged or narrowed arteries in the heart (coronary artery disease) are causing chest pain or a heart attack.If you have had a previous heart attack.How certain treatments for heart disease, such as a pacemaker, are working.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore \n\n\n        Contents\n      \n\n\n        Additional Services\n      \n\n\n        Prostate Blood Exam\n      \n\n\n\n\xa0\n\nProstate specific antigen, or PSA, is a protein produced by normal cells as well as malignant cells of the prostate gland. The PSA test measures the concentration of PSA in a man's blood. For this test, a blood sample is sent to a laboratory for analysis.Results are generally reported in nanograms of PSA per milliliter of blood (ng / ml). The concentration of PSA in the blood is frequently elevated in men with prostate cancer.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n What we offer \n Services \n\n\n\n\n\n\nDOT Physical \nmore info\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFamily     \n\n\n        Additional Services\n      \n\n\n        Antibiotic Injection\n      \n\n\n\n\xa0\n\nAn antibiotic is a chemical compound produced by some living beings\xa0(such as penicillin, which is produced by some species of fungi) or obtained through synthetic derivatives and that function as drugs that kill or inhibit the growth of bacteria, microorganisms sensitive to them.Each of the antibiotics used in medicine is aimed at treating an infection by a specific bacterium or group of bacteria.
